        <p class="date">
         Thu Apr 28, 2011 at 08:21 AM PDT
        </p>
        <h2>
         <a href="/story/2011/04/28/971018/-FL-Radio-Host-Arrested-at-Allen-West-Town-Hall-W-UPDATE-2-Nicole-Sandler-speaks-on-MSNBC" id="titleHref">
          FL Radio Host Arrested at Allen West "Town Hall" W/ UPDATE 2 - Nicole Sandler speaks on MSNBC
         </a>
         <span style="white-space: nowrap">
         </span>
        </h2>
        <p class="author">
         <span>
          by
         </span>
         <a href="/user/CodenameV">
          CodenameV
         </a>
         <a alt="Follow this author" class="ajax type-user do-hotlist do-updateContent size-tiny off altTooltip" href="#?friend_id=168490&amp;is_stream=1">
          Follow
         </a>
        </p>
        <ul class="front-page-share clearfix">
         <li style="margin-left: 0px">
          <div class="fb-share-button" data-href="http://www.dailykos.com/story/2011/04/28/971018/-FL-Radio-Host-Arrested-at-Allen-West-Town-Hall-W-UPDATE-2-Nicole-Sandler-speaks-on-MSNBC" data-layout="button_count">
          </div>
         </li>
         <li>
          <a class="twitter-share-button" data-count="horizontal" data-related="markos" data-text='FL Radio Host Arrested at Allen West "Town Hall" W/ UPDATE 2 - Nicole Sandler speaks on MSNBC' data-url="http://www.dailykos.com/story/2011/04/28/971018/-FL-Radio-Host-Arrested-at-Allen-West-Town-Hall-W-UPDATE-2-Nicole-Sandler-speaks-on-MSNBC" data-via="dailykos" href="https://twitter.com/share">
           Tweet
          </a>
         </li>
         <li>
          <a class="comments comment_count_with_new" data-comment_count="224" data-story_id="971018" href="/story/2011/04/28/971018/-FL-Radio-Host-Arrested-at-Allen-West-Town-Hall-W-UPDATE-2-Nicole-Sandler-speaks-on-MSNBC#comments">
           224 Comments
          </a>
         </li>
        </ul>
       </div>
       <div class="article-body">
        <div id="intro">
         <p>
          Florida Radio Host Nicole Sandler was arrested last night. The charge was Trespass after Warning. What was the actual charge? Asking her Congressman a follow-up question to a blatant lie regarding their Medicare privatization plan. Video and other details below the fold.
         </p>
        </div>
        <p class="divider-doodle">
        </p>
        <div class="article-body" id="body">
         <p>
          My title refers to a "Town Hall". The reason for the quotations indicate that only some folks would consider this a Town Hall. Reports indicate that the questions were hand picked by staffers ready-made with GOP talking points.
         </p>
         <p>
          Nicole Sandler herself, via
          <a href="http://digbysblog.blogspot.com/2011/04/constituent-service-arrest-and-mace-for.html">
           Digby
          </a>
          :
         </p>
         <blockquote>
          It figures, my blog is the last place youll read about my arrest and subsequent incarceration after attending Allen Wests so-called Town Hall Meeting last night.
          <p>
           Since I spent last night in jail and, thanks to the sickeningly awful people at the Broward County Jail was subjected to three hours in solitary confinement in a 710 room, and then maced. Nice, huh?
          </p>
          <p>
           Anyway, Ill have more on how it all unfolded on the show tomorrow, and then in a lengthier written piece after I get some rest, food and a shower.
          </p>
          <p>
           But I do want to clear something up. The video thats floating around portraying me as a heckler doesnt show the Medicare question that Mr. West was asked, the way he answered it, and my FOLLOW-UP question.
          </p>
          <p>
           So, heres how it actually happened:
          </p>
          <p>
           <iframe defang_allowfullscreen="" frameborder="0" height="349" src="http://www.youtube.com/embed/Dq8BEzknL3k" width="560">
           </iframe>
          </p>
          <p>
           Being arrested for speaking your mind at a political event is not unprecedented. I would guess that it's happened to a few of you. (It's not common to maced while in custody --- but I can't say I'm surprised that it happened to a female liberal talk show host. That's just how the authoritarians roll.)
          </p>
         </blockquote>
         <p>
          I'm also listening to her radio show. Following this video, she was physically assaulted by an officer, pushing her away from the "Town Hall". She was then informed that she was under arrest. All that was said was that she was under arrest for Trespass After Warning, and an audio recording of the incident quotes the police officer: "You don't have a say-so right now".
         </p>
         <p>
          She reports that she was not read her Miranda Rights, and spent the night in Jail, in solitary confinement. During her night in jail, she was reportedley MACED.
         </p>
         <p>
          I don't need to tell all of you that these actions are despicable. Not only are GOP congressman censoring questions that are being asked by constituents, but when met with any opposition, this is the treatment that she gets.
         </p>
         <p>
          She reports that, even in the back of the police car, while Allen West is posing for pictures with the officers next to the car, she is still asking "Congressman, can I please ask you a question?"
         </p>
         <p>
          Nicole Sandler, you are my hero today. I wish you the best of luck resolving this matter, and bringing to light the injustices of our democratic processes.
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           UPDATE:
          </strong>
          I would like to thank all of the folks recommending my diary, this is a serious issue, and hopefully in due time the local FL media wont be the only outlets covering this atrocity. I also want to thank mofembot, louisev, and others for catching some of the spelling/grammatical errors that were created in my haste.
         </p>
         <p>
          What we do know is that Nicole Sandler intends to pursue a lawsuit related to this matter. If you would like to help her with a legal fund, the donation page can be found
          <a href="http://radioornot.com/site/?page_id=3993">
           here
          </a>
          (thanks to Spedwybabs, who provided me the link and is
          <a href="http://www.dailykos.com/story/2011/04/27/970642/-Nicole-Sandler-ARRESTED-at-FL-Townhall-Last-Night!-WITH-UPDATES?showAll=yes">
           following this story as well
          </a>
          ).
         </p>
         <p>
          <strong>
           UPDATE 2:
          </strong>
          Video clip from Cenk on MSNBC (includes video of the arrest and interview with Nicole Sandler)
         </p>
         <p>
          <object classid="clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000" codebase="http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=10,0,0,0" height="245" id="msnbc66c733" width="420">

        <br/>
        <div>
         <p>
          Add keywords that describe this diary.
		Separate multiple keywords with commas.
          <br/>
          <a href="/special/tag_tips" target="_blank">
           Tagging tips
          </a>
          -
          <a href="/search?search_tags=1" target="_blank">
           Search For Tags
          </a>
          -
          <a href="http://www.dkosopedia.com/wiki/Tag:Tagfinder" target="_blank">
           Browse For Tags
          </a>
         </p>
         <div class="pageTip hasTooltip" style="margin-top:3px">
          ?
         </div>
         <div class="tooltipContents qtip-style-dk4_large qtip-pos-br">
          <p>
           <b>
            More Tagging tips:
           </b>
          </p>
          <p>
           A tag is a way to search for this diary. If someone is searching for "Barack Obama," is this a diary they'd be trying to find?
          </p>
          <p>
           Use a person's full name, without any title. Senator Obama may become President Obama, and Michelle Obama might run for office.
          </p>
          <p>
           If your diary covers an election or elected official, use election tags, which are generally the state abbreviation followed by the office. 
		CA-01 is the first district House seat. CA-Sen covers both senate races. NY-GOV covers the New York governor's race.
          </p>
          <p>
           Tags do not compound: that is, "education reform" is a completely different tag from "education". A tag like "reform" alone is probably not meaningful.
          </p>
         </div>
         <!-- &lt;h4 id="p_tagErrorMessage"&gt;You must enter at least one Tag for this Diary Entry:&lt;/h4&gt; -->
         <p>
          <input id="p_tagInput" name="tag_draft" size="70" type="text" value=""/>
          <!-- &lt;input id="tagSubmit" type="submit" name="submit" value="Submit" /&gt; -->
         </p>
         <p style="font-style:italic">
          Consider if one or more of these tags fits your diary:
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Civil Rights');return false;">
           Civil Rights
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Community');return false;">
           Community
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Congress');return false;">
           Congress
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Culture');return false;">
           Culture
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Economy');return false;">
           Economy
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Education');return false;">
           Education
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Elections');return false;">
           Elections
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Energy');return false;">
           Energy
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Environment');return false;">
           Environment
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Health Care');return false;">
           Health Care
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('International');return false;">
           International
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Labor');return false;">
           Labor
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Law');return false;">
           Law
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Media');return false;">
           Media
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Meta');return false;">
           Meta
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('National Security');return false;">
           National Security
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Science');return false;">
           Science
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Transportation');return false;">
           Transportation
          </a>
          , or
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('White House');return false;">
           White House
          </a>
          .
	If your diary is specific to a state, consider adding the state 
	(
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('California');return false;">
           California
          </a>
          ,
          <a href="#" onclick="addTagToField('Texas');return false;">
           Texas
          </a>
          , etc).
	Keep in mind, though, that there are many wonderful and important diaries
	that don't fit in any of these tags. Don't worry if yours doesn't.
         </p>

             <div class="ct">
              <p>
               I'm 60ish and always thought the GOPers were at the very worst lazy ideologues who drank martinis and had butlers to clean out the kitty litter box.
              </p>
              <p>
               When the republican party co-opted the religous right decades ago, allowed Rush Limbaugh to control the message then switched to 24/7 Fox, the end of what passed for sanity was predictable.
              </p>
              <p>
               Trump is the perfect face of today's republican party and despite my disgust for his recent performances, I'm delighted that his ignorance, greed, carnival barker persona and never ending desire for publicity put the republicans in exactly the right light.
              </p>

               anybody who is. Why don't you email the DKos Florida group. Maybe somebody in the group lives there and can post it. Or you can write a diary and ask a local to post it. As I noted above, I can republish to Florida group after you write it.
              </p>
             </div>
             <div class="cf">
              <p class="sig">
               I'm gay and I'm pissed. I'm not giving up, I'm not giving in, I'm not backing down, and I'm not going away. I'm one of the
               <a href="http://www.dailykos.com/blog/Angry%20Gays" rel="nofollow">
                Angry Gays
               </a>
               . Deal with it.
              </p>
              <p class="cb">
               by
               <a href="/user/uid:93403">

I'd happily listen to her, any day of the week, than any right wing voices out there (ugh. right wingers make me want to puke).
            <br/>
            When Randi isn't there (vaca, out sick, etc.), Nicole fills in. And I'm OK with that. And I have to say it was really interesting listening how it played out. I remember the show, earlier in the week, when she said her congressman was having a town hall and she was going. Then the proverbial "S" hit the fan!
            <br/>
            Nicole, or any American, deserves the treatment she got. I am ashamed to call myself an American from what I have seen.
            <br/>

            <br/>
            The right wing accuses the left of being authoritarian. Yeah, well, dudes? Look in the fucking mirror. We don't arrest people who exercise their American-given right to free speech.
            <br/>
            We are not the ones who created "Free Speech Zones".
            <br/>
            Goddam fucks.

  <script type="text/javascript">
   if($.cookie('meter_user') !== 'false') {
		if ($('#ePostButton').length &gt; 0) {
		  $('#ePostButton').click(function() { 
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Posted Comment', { 
		      repliedTo: $(this).parents('#eP').prevAll('.cb').children('a').first().html() 
		    });
		  });
		}
		
		if (!!document.location.pathname.match('activate') &amp;&amp; $('h1:contains("Welcome to Daily Kos!")').length &gt; 0) {
		  DailyKos.Metrics.track('Signed Up');
		}
		
		if (document.location.pathname === '/') {
		  if (document.location.hostname.match(/^www|^dailykos/)) {
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Front Page');
		  } else {
		    var subdomain = document.location.hostname.split('.')[0];
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Vertical', { name: subdomain });
		  }
		}
		
		if ($('.ratinate').length &gt; 0) {
		  $('.ratinate').click(function() { DailyKos.Metrics.track('Recommended Comment') });
		}
		
		if ($('.do-addRating.type-story').length &gt; 0) {
		  $('.do-addRating.type-story').click(function() { DailyKos.Metrics.track('Recommended Story') });
		}
		
		if ($("form[action$='publishHow']").length &gt; 0) {
		  $(document).ready(function() {
			  $('.type-story.do-publishHow').click(function() { DailyKos.Metrics.track('Published Story') });
			 });
		}
		
		if (document.location.pathname.match(/^\/user/) &amp;&amp; $('li.here').length &gt; 0) {
		  if ($('.pageMenu:first li.here').children('a').html().match(/Stream/)) {
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Stream', { name: $('.name').children('a').html() });
		  } else if ($('.pageMenu:first li.here').children('a').html().match(/Profile/)) {
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Profile', { name: $('.name').children('a').html() });
		  } else if ($('.pageMenu:last li.here').children('a').html().match(/My Recent Replies/)) {
		    DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Replies');
		  }
		} 
		
		if ($('#search-tabbed').length &gt; 0) {
		  DailyKos.Metrics.track('Searched');
		}
		
		if ($('#group-tables').length &gt; 0) {
			DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Groups List');
		}
		
		if (document.location.pathname.match(/^\/groups/) &amp;&amp; $("#group_info").length &gt; 0) {
		  DailyKos.Metrics.track('Viewed Group', { name: $('.name').children('a').text() });
		}
		
		if ($('.do-hotlist.type-user, .do-unHotlist.type-user').length &gt; 0) {
		  $('.do-hotlist.type-user, .do-unHotlist.type-user').click(function() {
		    var nickName;
		    nickName = ($(this).prev('a').html() || $('.name a').html())
		    if ($(this).hasClass('do-hotlist')) {
		      DailyKos.Metrics.track('Followed User', { nickname: nickName }) 
		    } else if ($(this).hasClass('do-unHotlist')) {
		      DailyKos.Metrics.track('Unfollowed User', { nickname: nickName }) 
		    }    
		  });
		}
	}
  </script>
